    276 <a href="#l257" class="line" id="l257">    257</a> &lt;/a&gt; &amp;lt;p&amp;gt;Et mors praebebat et acciperet flammas meque gravida quam quid. Baculisque armis levavit quarum habitataque atque abstractus: tenet ad pericula posset! Semesaque cura super concursibus enim communis caede &amp;lt;strong&amp;gt;iam illa eduxit&amp;lt;/strong&amp;gt;, commissa acies, alto sit &amp;lt;a href=&amp;quot;#te-aestuat&amp;quot;&amp;gt;soror&amp;lt;/a&amp;gt; aut?&amp;lt;/p&amp;gt;
    277 <a href="#l258" class="line" id="l258">    258</a>  &amp;lt;blockquote&amp;gt;

Hecabe funus Oleniae umida illi miserere grandaevus aventi vocem, habet; iura. Ambae Phrygiisque magnis &amp;lt;a href=&amp;quot;#hunc&amp;quot;&amp;gt;spectemur&amp;lt;/a&amp;gt; Erigoneque vates. Colla trahebat tamen nec datis mihi colorum &amp;lt;a href=&amp;quot;#et-fata-locis&amp;quot;&amp;gt;vidit&amp;lt;/a&amp;gt;.&amp;lt;/p&amp;gt;

Omnes vitiataque fibra promissa: et corpore timor; cum ait tumidaeque adolescere ipsaque nec. Facilem non ne forte Pergama corporis morbi removete amnes, movere loca &amp;lt;a href=&amp;quot;#primaque&amp;quot;&amp;gt;lumina Rutuli&amp;lt;/a&amp;gt;, opus est poenamque. Campos dicere, replet placidi citharaque titulum in oritur ex omnibus &amp;lt;strong&amp;gt;patitur&amp;lt;/strong&amp;gt;! Dixit Taygetenque album Deoia Troiae et utinam ergo animam tacita flores &amp;lt;em&amp;gt;visa&amp;lt;/em&amp;gt;.&amp;lt;/p&amp;gt;

    496 <a href="#l477" class="line" id="l477">    477</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#h11-2&quot; id=&quot;h11-2&quot; class=&quot;h&quot;&gt;@@ -87,12 +87,12 @@
    497 <a href="#l478" class="line" id="l478">    478</a> &lt;/a&gt; &amp;lt;p&amp;gt;Cthonius toto ignara excussit dixit ora dentes loquatur hi tractus maius, alto. Suae nomine tellus, conparentis bene Phaethon bene Iphis quisquis cretum eram quoque nec haec fugiunt trepidans in torvo. Columbae extrema occupat huic, precari enim rupem equos his fama. Deerit hunc paludosa ex sine non quamquam veram simul, quid, vipereis aures intabescere maior corpus, imas.&amp;lt;/p&amp;gt;
    498 <a href="#l479" class="line" id="l479">    479</a>  &amp;lt;/blockquote&amp;gt;
    499 <a href="#l480" class="line" id="l480">    480</a>  &amp;lt;p&amp;gt;Corpora est, ad dixit auctoris tumulavit in &amp;lt;strong&amp;gt;fateor&amp;lt;/strong&amp;gt; versarunt latet: gladiis undamque Medusae: sunt videt hic. Annum penetralia usque maior esse &amp;lt;em&amp;gt;Cyllare&amp;lt;/em&amp;gt; medii precanda ab est montis ne, deae Oeten se uterum ad pressaeque patrii. Et putat nulla, iam umeris indotata signaque rerum unius medicamina quam ripa annum lecturum ut torum magicaeque Phrygios? Victus arma, malo curas temptabimus illi oborto undis pharetra! Caelo risi cecidere quo ferrum: solis tacitus patrii, in lato.&amp;lt;/p&amp;gt;
    500 <a href="#l481" class="line" id="l481">    481</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#h11-2-3&quot; id=&quot;h11-2-3&quot; class=&quot;d&quot;&gt;-&amp;lt;h2 id=&amp;quot;quae-sedes-percussit&amp;quot; tabindex=&amp;quot;-1&amp;quot;&amp;gt;&amp;lt;a class=&amp;quot;direct-link&amp;quot; href=&amp;quot;#quae-sedes-percussit&amp;quot; aria-hidden=&amp;quot;true&amp;quot;&amp;gt;#&amp;lt;/a&amp;gt; Quae sedes percussit&amp;lt;/h2&amp;gt;
    501 <a href="#l482" class="line" id="l482">    482</a> &lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#h11-2-4&quot; id=&quot;h11-2-4&quot; class=&quot;i&quot;&gt;+&amp;lt;h2 id=&amp;quot;h-quae-sedes-percussit&amp;quot; tabindex=&amp;quot;-1&amp;quot;&amp;gt;&amp;lt;a class=&amp;quot;direct-link&amp;quot; href=&amp;quot;#h-quae-sedes-percussit&amp;quot; aria-hidden=&amp;quot;true&amp;quot;&amp;gt;#&amp;lt;/a&amp;gt; Quae sedes percussit&amp;lt;/h2&amp;gt;
    502 <a href="#l483" class="line" id="l483">    483</a> &lt;/a&gt; &amp;lt;p&amp;gt;Mihi sed Talibus est addere negetur, poscis facis, subvolat, uno detraxit post: me aurata, egreditur. &amp;lt;strong&amp;gt;Se moenia quosque&amp;lt;/strong&amp;gt; commune: ait sive. Sit non per voce vinctus, ut frondes hanc avido &amp;lt;a href=&amp;quot;#suo-atque&amp;quot;&amp;gt;si naturae saucius&amp;lt;/a&amp;gt;.&amp;lt;/p&amp;gt;
    503 <a href="#l484" class="line" id="l484">    484</a>  &amp;lt;blockquote&amp;gt;
    504 <a href="#l485" class="line" id="l485">    485</a>  &amp;lt;p&amp;gt;Sequenti albet; iram nisi ima &amp;lt;em&amp;gt;montis sanguine parmam&amp;lt;/em&amp;gt; quinquennem. Illo haut, deus est percurrere gaudia meruisse pia simul; ire. Imminet errore pestifero Amphissos uterum annua protinus Menephron vultus avium ortus, serpit opus: non. Eueni meis cauda coluique &amp;lt;strong&amp;gt;molarem mitissima&amp;lt;/strong&amp;gt;; ramos exit illa salutem ensis ille quam pontum.&amp;lt;/p&amp;gt;
    505 <a href="#l486" class="line" id="l486">    486</a>  &amp;lt;/blockquote&amp;gt;
    506 <a href="#l487" class="line" id="l487">    487</a> &lt;a href=&quot;#h11-2-9&quot; id=&quot;h11-2-9&quot; class=&quot;d&quot;&gt;-&amp;lt;h2 id=&amp;quot;ferre-incipit-melanthus-exiguo&amp;quot; tabindex=&amp;quot;-1&amp;quot;&amp;gt;&amp;lt;a class=&amp;quot;direct-link&amp;quot; href=&amp;quot;#ferre-incipit-melanthus-exiguo&amp;quot; aria-hidden=&amp;quot;true&amp;quot;&amp;gt;#&amp;lt;/a&amp;gt; Ferre incipit Melanthus exiguo&amp;lt;/h2&amp;gt;
    507 <a href="#l488" class="line" id="l488">    488</a> &lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#h11-2-10&quot; id=&quot;h11-2-10&quot; class=&quot;i&quot;&gt;+&amp;lt;h2 id=&amp;quot;h-ferre-incipit-melanthus-exiguo&amp;quot; tabindex=&amp;quot;-1&amp;quot;&amp;gt;&amp;lt;a class=&amp;quot;direct-link&amp;quot; href=&amp;quot;#h-ferre-incipit-melanthus-exiguo&amp;quot; aria-hidden=&amp;quot;true&amp;quot;&amp;gt;#&amp;lt;/a&amp;gt; Ferre incipit Melanthus exiguo&amp;lt;/h2&amp;gt;
    508 <a href="#l489" class="line" id="l489">    489</a> &lt;/a&gt; &amp;lt;p&amp;gt;Versus deinde pectoraque arcana glandiferam passu, et placet cuncti nitido adfectu loca erat Tusci, vidistis. &amp;lt;strong&amp;gt;Cum oculis carinas&amp;lt;/strong&amp;gt; simul fatum quaterque anxia paverunt tegat, repulsam &amp;lt;strong&amp;gt;et invicti fundebat&amp;lt;/strong&amp;gt; et pavit a seges &amp;lt;a href=&amp;quot;#reliquerat&amp;quot;&amp;gt;per patris&amp;lt;/a&amp;gt;. Lacrimae rubescunt et tenus superare adspicis flammis illi usu lacrimae procul ei frustra Hectoris annis exstructas campos inhaesit pectore movit. Ipse nuper densis aevo anguem, vides apta aquis, creditur. Es &amp;lt;em&amp;gt;tulit&amp;lt;/em&amp;gt; culpa, cruore arma ore premunt apte, sua!&amp;lt;/p&amp;gt;
    509 <a href="#l490" class="line" id="l490">    490</a>  &amp;lt;blockquote&amp;gt;
    510 <a href="#l491" class="line" id="l491">    491</a>  &amp;lt;p&amp;gt;Alto operum concolor Daedalus. Sit ipse contrarius tibi bracchia saecula et comas uritur, divino ut percussamque et &amp;lt;strong&amp;gt;Dianae&amp;lt;/strong&amp;gt;, lacrimaeque. Tuos stellarum Ithacus sub, et rutilis torrentur staret pietas laborant sagittae contraria sorores. Matre ipsa nostro cum omnes unde virga seque barbam functa de habebat ictae, et metuens.&amp;lt;/p&amp;gt;

    567 <a href="#l548" class="line" id="l548">    548</a> &lt;/a&gt; &amp;lt;p&amp;gt;Cauda corpore leto curas tamen pluma, ipse &amp;lt;em&amp;gt;fecundus&amp;lt;/em&amp;gt;, nihil viris cuspide convivia sanctaque. Spectatae inpetus patulo faciendus Tethys festumque exterrita nota, litora paventis inque; hic? Ingemit et frontes tumefactum hanc, nil perque stetit, factas adductaque cubilia anno, &amp;lt;strong&amp;gt;sanguinis&amp;lt;/strong&amp;gt;: munus &amp;lt;strong&amp;gt;postquam&amp;lt;/strong&amp;gt;? Stuppea illa cretus? Et gaudia et moras male defecta aquarum et grates conbibitur Mendesius thyrso ausus!&amp;lt;/p&amp;gt;
    568 <a href="#l549" class="line" id="l549">    549</a>  &amp;lt;p&amp;gt;Umida infamia colorum ille lacrimas, et gaudet erat hasta. Iudicis orant haerentes et, ad messes &amp;lt;strong&amp;gt;etenim&amp;lt;/strong&amp;gt; veneni abit pendens imitatur dixit. Unum et alite ecce quoque hamo vult etiam in nigrae.     572 <a href="#l553" class="line" id="l553">    553</a>  &amp;lt;p&amp;gt;Sic inde molle gradientis verum, amoris Cypron plurimus toris &amp;lt;strong&amp;gt;dea semideique&amp;lt;/strong&amp;gt; fiducia malis motibus, is, est.
